â€œWe will show them Our signs in the universe and in their own selves, until it becomes manifest to them that this (the Quran) is the truthâ€ (Quran; 41:53).  In Surah Al-Anbya, Allah (SWT) also states: â€œHave those who disbelieved not considered that the heavens and the earth were a joined entity, and We separated themâ€ (Quran, 21:30). In 1929, American astronomer Edwin Hubble proposed the Hubbleâ€™s Law according to which all entities in space are moving away from the Earth at speeds proportional to their distance i.e. the greater the distance from earth, the faster they are moving. Soon after this, he discovered that galaxies are moving away from each other as well which means that the universe is expanding overall.  This laid the basis for the Big Bang theory which states that around 12-15 billion years ago the universe came into existence from one single extremely hot and dense point, due to an explosion of this point the universe came into being. The universe, since then, has been expanding from this single point. In 1965, radio astronomers Arno Penzias and Robert Wilson won the Noble Prize for the discovery that confirmed the Big Bang theory. When looking at the verse cited above, while acknowledging Allah Knows best, it remains astounding that the Quran had already revealed that â€œthe heavens and the earth were a joined entity, and We separated themâ€  Again, in Surah Al-Anbya, Allah (SWT) says: â€œThe Day when We will fold the heaven like the folding of a [written] sheet for the records. As We began the first creation, We will repeat it. [That is] a promise binding upon Us. Indeed, We will do itâ€ (Quran, 21:104). This fits in with the theory of Big Crunch which talks about how the universe will be pulled back into the black holes and again form a tiny mass.  In Surah Al-Anbya, Allah (SWT) says: â€œAnd We made the sky a protected ceiling, but they, from its signs, are turning awayâ€ (Quran 21:32). It is a scientific fact that the sky, with all of its gasses, protects the earth and life that is present on it from the harmful rays of the sun. If there was no protective layer, life on earth would cease to exist as the temperature on earth would be freezing at -270.556Â°C, the same as the temperature in space.  In Surah Al-Anbya, it states â€œAnd it is He who created the night and the day and the sun and the moon; all [heavenly bodies] in an orbit are swimmingâ€ (Quran, 21:33). Although it was only a widespread belief in the 20th century amongst the astronomers, today it is a well-established fact that the Sun, the Moon, and all the other bodies in the Universe are moving in an orbit and constantly moving, not stationary as commonly thought before.   This and many other scientific miracles from the Quran could not have been known 1444 years ago by any human beings.

It's bittersweet for me. In time where authenticity in rap is scarce I discovered Ralo. I didn't listen to his music because he was the best rapper. I began listening to him because he seemed authentic and I could intimately relate to the position he operated from.  However, now I cannot bring myself to fully support the brother due to the unresolved paperwork situation. Regardless if he never took the stand and testified or was merely fabricating evidence to subvert being incarcerated. The oath where WE come from forbids us from sitting down with ANY law enforcement official to proffer evidenceâ€“be it real or fakeâ€“that could potentially incriminate another.  That's what lawyers are for. And if you're going to go that route, then you let the people whom you're paying to take the case come forward and speak to the law officialsâ€“that's what you're paying them to do.  That said, if what brother Ralo says is TRUTH, then file a request with the court to unseal all statements and documents involved in the case in question. Be completely transparent my brother. This will remove any and all taint of the alleged transgression.  Here is a passage from the Hadith. The Prophet said this after visiting a market place and sticking his hand into a heap of corn that a trader was selling, only to discover the corn below was wet:  Why did you not keep the wet portion above the dry corn, so that people may see it? He who deceives is not one of us.â€  Those traders who cheat customers (us the music consumer) by not showing the true product (you the artist) or hiding flaws of the product they are offering, from their customers are not among the true Muslims according to the judgment of Prophet Muhammad.   My brother Ralo, I am not passing judgment. This comes from a place of love. As muslim you must stand firmly in Islam and let it guide you completely.
